def extract_audio(video_path, audio_path):
    command = [
        "ffmpeg", "-i", video_path,
        "-ac", "1", "-ar", "16000",
        "-vn", "-y", audio_path
    ]
    subprocess.run(command, check=True)

def unload_model(model):

    torch.cuda.empty_cache()

from locust import HttpUser, task, between

class WebsiteUser(HttpUser):
    wait_time = between(1, 5)

    @task
    def dubbing_task(self):
        self.client.post("/api/upload", files={'file': open('test.mp4', 'rb')})
        self.client.post("/api/dubbing", json={'target_lang': 'ja'})

python
def verify_payment(imp_uid, merchant_uid):
    token = get_admin_token()
    payment_data = requests.get(f"https://api.iamport.kr/payments/{imp_uid}", headers=...).json()
    
    order = db.query(Order).filter_by(id=merchant_uid).first()
    if payment_data['amount'] == order.amount:
        order.status = 'paid'
        user.credits += order.credits
        db.commit()

def get_order(order_id: int, current_user: User):
    order = db.query(Order).get(order_id)
    if order.user_id != current_user.id:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Not authorized")
    return order

def create_invitation_link(team_id, email):
    token = create_access_token(data={"sub": email, "team_id": team_id}, expires_delta=timedelta(hours=24))
    return f"{BASE_URL}/invite?token={token}"

RBAC ?곗퐫?덉씠??

python
def require_role(role: str):
    def decorator(func):
        @wraps(func)
        def wrapper(args, kwargs):
            if current_user.role != role:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=403)
            return func(args, kwargs)
        return wrapper
    return decorator

from botocore.signers import CloudFrontSigner

def rsa_signer(message):
    with open('private_key.pem', 'rb') as key_file:
        private_key = serialization.load_pem_private_key(key_file.read(), password=None)
    return private_key.sign(message, padding.PKCS1v15(), hashes.SHA1())

signer = CloudFrontSigner(key_id, rsa_signer)
url = signer.generate_presigned_url(url, date_less_than=expire_date)

Celery Task

python
@celery_app.task(bind=True, max_retries=3)
def send_email_task(self, to_email, subject, body):
    try:
        ses.send_email(...)
    except Exception as e:
        self.retry(exc=e, countdown=60)

    process_pipeline(job_id)
except Exception as e:
    logger.error(f"Job {job_id} failed: {e}")
    job.status = "Failed"
    job.error_message = str(e)
finally:
    cleanup_temp_files(job_id)

SQLAlchemy 紐⑤뜽

python
class Glossary(Base):
    __tablename__ = "glossaries"
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    user_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("users.id"))
    name = Column(String)
    source_lang = Column(String)
    target_lang = Column(String)
    terms = relationship("GlossaryTerm", back_populates="glossary")

class GlossaryTerm(Base):
    __tablename__ = "glossary_terms"
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    glossary_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("glossaries.id"))
    source_term = Column(String)
    target_term = Column(String)

Python Logic

python
parts = []
last_end = 0
for seg in segments:
    # ?먮낯 援ш컙 (?욌?遺?
    parts.append(trim_video(original, last_end, seg['start']))
    # ?붾튃 援ш컙
    dubbed_part = process_pipeline(trim_video(original, seg['start'], seg['end']))
    parts.append(dubbed_part)
    last_end = seg['end']
?⑥? ?룸?遺?
parts.append(trim_video(original, last_end, duration))
蹂묓빀
final = concat_videos(parts)
